//welcome to my bunny-buddy code!
//taking care of bunny-buddy is simple. Play with and feed bunny to keep him happy. But dont neglect him for too long....(he's clingy!)
#define SSD1306_NO_SPLASH

#include <CuteBuzzerSounds.h>
#include <Sounds.h>

#include <SPI.h>
#include <Wire.h>
#include <Adafruit_GFX.h>
#include <Adafruit_SSD1306.h>

#define SCREEN_WIDTH 128
#define SCREEN_HEIGHT 64
#define OLED_RESET 4

Adafruit_SSD1306 display(SCREEN_WIDTH, SCREEN_HEIGHT, &Wire, OLED_RESET);

#define BUZZER_PIN 7
#define BUTTON_EAT 2   // Pin for feed action
#define BUTTON_LOVE 4  // Pin for pet action


// Animation config
#define FRAME_DURATION   500UL    // ms between frames
#define IDLE_DURATION    10000UL  // ms in idle state
#define ALERT_DURATION   10000UL  // ms in alert state
#define CRY_DURATION     20000UL //  ms in cry state
#define EAT_DURATION     4000UL //  ms in eat state
#define LOVE_DURATION    6000UL //  ms in love state
#define GAMEOVER_DURATION 

#define NUM_FRAMES_IDLE  3
#define NUM_FRAMES_ALERT 3
#define NUM_FRAMES_CRY 4
#define NUM_FRAMES_EAT 7
#define NUM_FRAMES_LOVE 6
#define NUM_FRAMES_GAMEOVER 3

	0x00, 0x00, 0x00, 0x00, 0x00, 0x0c, 0x00, 0x30, 0x30, 0x00, 0xc0, 0x00, 0x00, 0x00, 0x00, 0x00, 
	0x00, 0x00, 0x00, 0x00, 0x00, 0x0c, 0x00, 0x30, 0x30, 0x00, 0xc0, 0x00, 0x00, 0x00, 0x00, 0x00, 
	0x00, 0x00, 0x00, 0x00, 0x00, 0x0c, 0x00, 0x00, 0x00, 0x00, 0xc0, 0x00, 0x00, 0x00, 0x00, 0x00, 
	0x00, 0x00, 0x00, 0x00, 0x00, 0x0c, 0x00, 0x00, 0x00, 0x00, 0xc0, 0x00, 0x00, 0x00, 0x00, 0x00
};
//told you it was long

// Convenience arrays so it knows which frames are for which animations
const unsigned char* const IDLE_FRAMES[NUM_FRAMES_IDLE] = { frame0, frame1, frame2 };
const unsigned char* const ALERT_FRAMES[NUM_FRAMES_ALERT] = { frame3, frame4, frame5 };
const unsigned char* const CRY_FRAMES[NUM_FRAMES_CRY] = {frame6, frame7, frame8, frame9};
const unsigned char* const EAT_FRAMES[NUM_FRAMES_EAT] = {frame10, frame11, frame12, frame13, frame14, frame15, frame16};
const unsigned char* const LOVE_FRAMES[NUM_FRAMES_LOVE] = {frame17, frame18 ,frame19 ,frame20 , frame21, frame22};
const unsigned char* const GAMEOVER_FRAMES[NUM_FRAMES_GAMEOVER] = {frame23, frame24, frame25};

// -------------------- State --------------------
enum Mode { MODE_IDLE, MODE_ALERT, MODE_CRY, MODE_EAT, MODE_LOVE, MODE_GAMEOVER };
Mode mode = MODE_IDLE;

uint8_t currentFrame = 0;
unsigned long lastFrameTime = 0;
unsigned long stateStartTime = 0;

// Sound control flags
bool playedSound = false;

void showFrame(const unsigned char* bmp) {
  display.clearDisplay();
  display.drawBitmap(0, 0, bmp, SCREEN_WIDTH, SCREEN_HEIGHT, SSD1306_WHITE);
  display.display();
}

void changeState(Mode newMode) {
  mode = newMode;
  stateStartTime = millis();
  currentFrame = 0;
  playedSound = false;
}

bool buttonPressed(int pin) {
  return digitalRead(pin) == LOW;
}

void setup() {
  Wire.begin();
  if (!display.begin(SSD1306_SWITCHCAPVCC, 0x3C)) {
    for (;;) {}
  }
  display.clearDisplay();
  display.display();

  pinMode(BUTTON_EAT, INPUT_PULLUP);
  pinMode(BUTTON_LOVE, INPUT_PULLUP);

  cute.init(BUZZER_PIN);
  changeState(MODE_IDLE);
  lastFrameTime = millis();
}

void loop() {
  unsigned long now = millis();

  // Handle button input 
  bool eatPressed = buttonPressed(BUTTON_EAT);
  bool lovePressed = buttonPressed(BUTTON_LOVE);

  // State logic
  switch (mode) {
    case MODE_IDLE:
      if (eatPressed) changeState(MODE_EAT);
      else if (lovePressed) changeState(MODE_LOVE);
      else if (now - stateStartTime >= IDLE_DURATION) changeState(MODE_ALERT);
      break;

    case MODE_ALERT:
      if (eatPressed) changeState(MODE_EAT);
      else if (lovePressed) changeState(MODE_LOVE);
      else if (now - stateStartTime >= ALERT_DURATION) changeState(MODE_CRY);
      break;

    case MODE_CRY:
      if (eatPressed) changeState(MODE_EAT);
      else if (lovePressed) changeState(MODE_LOVE);
      else if (now - stateStartTime >= CRY_DURATION) changeState(MODE_GAMEOVER);
      break;

    case MODE_EAT:
      if (now - stateStartTime >= EAT_DURATION) changeState(MODE_IDLE);
      break;

    case MODE_LOVE:
      if (now - stateStartTime >= LOVE_DURATION) changeState(MODE_IDLE);
      break;

    case MODE_GAMEOVER:
      if (eatPressed || lovePressed) changeState(MODE_IDLE);
      break;
  }

  // --- Play sounds ---
  if (!playedSound) {
    switch (mode) {
      case MODE_IDLE: cute.play(S_CUDDLY); break;
      case MODE_ALERT: cute.play(S_SURPRISE); break;
      case MODE_CRY: cute.play(S_SAD); break;
      case MODE_EAT: cute.play(S_HAPPY); break;
      case MODE_LOVE: cute.play(S_MODE1); break;
      case MODE_GAMEOVER: cute.play(S_OHOOH); break;
    }
    playedSound = true;
  }

  // --- Animation frame update ---
  if (now - lastFrameTime >= FRAME_DURATION) {
    lastFrameTime = now;
    switch (mode) {
      case MODE_IDLE:
        currentFrame = (currentFrame + 1) % NUM_FRAMES_IDLE;
        showFrame(IDLE_FRAMES[currentFrame]);
        break;
      case MODE_ALERT:
        currentFrame = (currentFrame + 1) % NUM_FRAMES_ALERT;
        showFrame(ALERT_FRAMES[currentFrame]);
        break;
      case MODE_CRY:
        currentFrame = (currentFrame + 1) % NUM_FRAMES_CRY;
        showFrame(CRY_FRAMES[currentFrame]);
        break;
      case MODE_EAT:
        currentFrame = (currentFrame + 1) % NUM_FRAMES_EAT;
        showFrame(EAT_FRAMES[currentFrame]);
        break;
      case MODE_LOVE:
        currentFrame = (currentFrame + 1) % NUM_FRAMES_LOVE;
        showFrame(LOVE_FRAMES[currentFrame]);
        break;
      case MODE_GAMEOVER:
        currentFrame = (currentFrame + 1) % NUM_FRAMES_GAMEOVER;
        showFrame(GAMEOVER_FRAMES[currentFrame]);
        break;
    }
  }
}
